about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2><p>This lecture continues
  to explore factor markets, using minimum wage and the labor market as examples.
  See <a href="./resolveuid/e4635a413517f55c518f491dae1f8f0a">Handout 16</a> for relevant
  graphs for this lecture.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Prof. Jonathan
  Gruber</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p>

  <span m="638560">in</span> <span m="638710">a</span> <span m="638740">market</span>
  <span m="639640">where</span> <span m="639730">you</span> <span m="639790">could</span>
  <span m="639910">literally</span> <span m="640330">shop</span> <span m="640780">costlessly</span>
  <span m="641410">across</span> <span m="641740">all</span> <span m="641890">the</span>
  <span m="642010">people</span> <span m="642370">selling</span> <span m="642760">their</span>
  <span m="642880">little</span> <span m="643390">fake</span> <span m="644080">Eiffel</span>
  <span m="644350">towers,</span> <span m="645400">little</span> <span m="645610">statue</span>
  <span m="646080">Eiffel</span> <span m="646220">towers.</span> <span m="646450">And
  you</span> <span m="646540">could</span> <span m="646660">perfectly</span> <span

  <span m="648880">carpet.</span> <span m="650170">There</span> <span m="650290">was</span>
  <span m="650440">full</span> <span m="650710">information.</span> <span m="651250">The</span>
  <span m="651310">prices</span> <span m="651640">were</span> <span m="651760">posted.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="659680">Any</span> <span m="659920">given</span> <span m="660160">firm,</span>

  <span m="669310">buy</span> <span m="669520">it.</span></p><p><span m="670420">Well,</span>

  <span m="674870">So</span> <span m="674890">I want</span> <span m="674990">to</span>

  <span m="675520">it.</span> <span m="676240">When</span> <span m="676390">we're</span>

  <span m="831620">able</span> <span m="831740">to</span> <span m="831800">get</span>

  <span m="836660">this</span> <span m="836810">is</span> <span m="836930">very</span>
  <span m="837320">much</span> <span m="837530">parallel</span> <span m="837920">to</span>
  <span m="838040">monopoly.</span> <span m="838880">In</span> <span m="838970">fact,</span>
  <span m="839240">we</span> <span m="839360">call</span> <span m="839750">this</span>
  <span m="840520">a</span> <span m="840620">monopsony.</span> <span m="844990">A</span>

  <span m="846860">labor</span> <span m="847340">market</span> <span m="848120">where</span>
  <span m="848300">firms</span> <span m="848810">have</span> <span m="848990">market</span>
  <span m="849320">power</span> <span m="849740">over</span> <span m="849980">workers</span>
  <span m="851270">just</span> <span m="851480">like</span> <span m="851630">a</span>
  <span m="851690">monopoly</span> <span m="852950">is</span> <span m="853130">a</span>
  <span m="853190">goods</span> <span m="853610">market</span> <span m="854540">where</span>
  <span m="854690">firms</span> <span m="855110">have</span> <span m="855230">market</span>
  <span m="855500">power</span> <span m="855860">over</span> <span m="856040">consumers.</span>
  <span m="858800">Now,</span> <span m="858980">this</span> <span m="859220">is</span>
  <span m="859340">not</span> <span m="859550">so</span> <span m="859730">crazy.</span>
  <span m="860900">And</span> <span m="861050">in</span> <span m="861140">fact,</span>
  <span m="861920">it</span> <span m="862040">applies</span> <span m="862460">very</span>
  <span m="862730">much</span> <span m="862970">to</span> <span m="863090">me.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="865670">situation</span> <span m="866230">at</span> <span m="866340">MIT.</span>

  <span m="1494160">That's</span> <span m="1494280">a</span> <span m="1494340">great</span>
  <span m="1494520">question.</span> <span m="1495100">So</span> <span m="1495150">what</span>

  <span m="1664130">all</span> <span m="1664250">forms</span> <span m="1664550">of</span>

  <span m="1679700">going</span> <span m="1679910">to</span> <span m="1679970">the</span>
  <span m="1680060">capital</span> <span m="1680480">market,</span> <span m="1682310">which</span>
  <span m="1682550">is</span> <span m="1682670">basically</span> <span m="1683090">the</span>

  <span m="1684650">that</span> <span m="1684810">firms</span> <span m="1685250">can</span>

  <span m="1692980">over,</span> <span m="1693220">and</span> <span m="1693310">there's</span>
  <span m="1693460">a</span> <span m="1693520">big</span> <span m="1693700">pool</span>
  <span m="1694000">of</span> <span m="1694090">money.</span> <span m="1694860">And</span>
  <span m="1694990">I</span> <span m="1695050">have</span> <span m="1695170">to</span>
  <span m="1695260">take</span> <span m="1695500">the</span> <span m="1695590">money</span>

  <span m="1701780">And</span> <span m="1701930">where</span> <span m="1702260">does</span>
  <span m="1702440">the</span> <span m="1702530">money</span> <span m="1702860">in</span>

  <span m="1703670">from?</span> <span m="1705320">It</span> <span m="1705420">comes</span>
  <span m="1706180">from</span> <span m="1706450">household</span> <span m="1707170">savings</span>
  <span m="1707740">decisions.</span></p><p><span m="1709940">So</span> <span m="1710050">the</span>
  <span m="1710140">capital</span> <span m="1710740">market</span> <span m="1711610">is</span>
  <span m="1711790">a</span> <span m="1711850">market</span> <span m="1712180">where</span>
  <span m="1712330">the</span> <span m="1712390">demand</span> <span m="1712990">for</span>
  <span m="1713170">capital</span> <span m="1714770">comes</span> <span m="1716330">from</span>
  <span m="1716570">firm's</span> <span m="1718010">interest</span> <span m="1718520">in</span>
  <span m="1718670">investing</span> <span m="1720080">and</span> <span m="1720200">having</span>
  <span m="1720500">more</span> <span m="1720710">in</span> <span m="1720800">the</span>
  <span m="1720860">future.</span> <span m="1722030">The</span> <span m="1722190">supply</span>
  <span m="1722780">of</span> <span m="1722870">capital</span> <span m="1723740">comes</span>
  <span m="1724190">from</span> <span m="1724370">people's</span> <span m="1724970">decisions</span>
  <span m="1725510">to</span> <span m="1725600">save.</span> <span m="1727110">And</span>
  <span m="1727260">essentially,</span> <span m="1728160">the</span> <span m="1728280">money</span>
  <span m="1728760">firms</span> <span m="1729240">use</span> <span m="1730110">to</span>
  <span m="1730230">buy</span> <span m="1730560">stuff</span> <span m="1731490">is</span>
  <span m="1731700">borrowed</span> <span m="1732270">from</span> <span m="1732510">people.</span>
  <span m="1734010">And</span> <span m="1734130">that's</span> <span m="1734490">the</span>
  <span m="1734580">bottom</span> <span m="1734970">line</span> <span m="1735180">of</span>
  <span m="1735240">how</span> <span m="1735360">capital</span> <span m="1735720">markets</span>
  <span m="1736050">work.</span></p><p><span m="1737780">So</span> <span m="1737920">just</span>
  <span m="1738520">as</span> <span m="1741250">the</span> <span m="1741370">supply</span>
  <span m="1741880">of</span> <span m="1742000">labor</span> <span m="1743200">that</span>
  <span m="1743320">determines</span> <span m="1743800">how</span> <span m="1743950">many</span>
  <span m="1744160">workers</span> <span m="1744670">a</span> <span m="1744730">firm</span>

  <span m="1747070">of</span> <span m="1747160">how</span> <span m="1747340">hard</span>
  <span m="1747520">to</span> <span m="1747670">work,</span> <span m="1748870">the</span>
  <span m="1748990">supply</span> <span m="1749410">of</span> <span m="1749530">capital</span>
  <span m="1750610">that</span> <span m="1750760">determines</span> <span m="1751180">how</span>
  <span m="1751300">many</span> <span m="1751450">machines</span> <span m="1751940">a</span>

  <span m="1755440">hard</span> <span m="1755680">to</span> <span m="1755770">save.</span>
  <span m="1758060">So</span> <span m="1758210">let's</span> <span m="1758480">look</span>
  <span m="1758630">at</span> <span m="1758720">figure</span> <span m="1758970">16-5,</span>
  <span m="1760400">equilibrium</span> <span m="1760910">in</span> <span m="1761000">capital</span>

  <span m="1932560">implicitly</span> <span m="1933700">I</span> <span m="1933940">loan</span>
  <span m="1934210">money</span> <span m="1934450">to</span> <span m="1934540">firms.</span></p><p><span
  m="1936820">The</span> <span m="1936910">first</span> <span m="1937390">is</span>
  <span m="1938560">I</span> <span m="1938680">could</span> <span m="1938890">literally</span>
  <span m="1940870">buy</span> <span m="1941170">corporate</span> <span m="1942760">debt.</span>
  <span m="1944090">I</span> <span m="1944110">could</span> <span m="1944320">literally</span>
  <span m="1945160">loan</span> <span m="1945640">the</span> <span m="1945730">money</span>
  <span m="1946000">to</span> <span m="1946150">firms.</span> <span m="1947790">I</span>
  <span m="1947910">could</span> <span m="1948030">literally</span> <span m="1948870">go</span>
  <span m="1949320">and</span> <span m="1949440">the</span> <span m="1949500">firm</span>
  <span m="1949770">could</span> <span m="1949920">say,</span> <span m="1950310">I,</span>
  <span m="1950910">General</span> <span m="1951240">Motors,</span> <span m="1952650">am</span>
  <span m="1952950">issuing</span> <span m="1953400">a</span> <span m="1953460">bond.</span>
  <span m="1954270">This</span> <span m="1954450">is</span> <span m="1954570">through</span>
  <span m="1954720">bond,</span> <span m="1955140">issuing</span> <span m="1955470">a</span>
  <span m="1955530">bond.</span></p><p><span m="1955980">And</span> <span m="1956100">the</span>
  <span m="1956190">way</span> <span m="1956310">that</span> <span m="1956430">bond</span>
  <span m="1956700">works</span> <span m="1957390">is</span> <span m="1957690">I</span>
  <span m="1957870">promise</span> <span m="1958860">that</span> <span m="1959010">for</span>
  <span m="1959100">every</span> <span m="1959280">dollar</span> <span m="1959610">you</span>
  <span m="1959760">spend</span> <span m="1960030">buying</span> <span m="1960300">my</span>
  <span m="1960450">bond,</span> <span m="1961080">you'll</span> <span m="1961260">get</span>
  <span m="1961440">1</span> <span m="1961740">plus</span> <span m="1962070">I</span>
  <span m="1962280">dollars</span> <span m="1962640">back</span> <span m="1963990">at</span>
  <span m="1964080">the</span> <span m="1964230">end--</span> <span m="1966160">or</span>
  <span m="1966460">next</span> <span m="1966730">year,</span> <span m="1966910">say,</span>
  <span m="1967570">depends on</span> <span m="1967840">how long</span> <span m="1968110">the

  <span m="1970120">money</span> <span m="1970360">to</span> <span m="1970420">the</span>
  <span m="1970510">firm</span> <span m="1970870">by</span> <span m="1971080">buying--</span>
  <span m="1971590">you're</span> <span m="1971740">buying</span> <span m="1972070">their</span>
  <span m="1972250">promise</span> <span m="1972730">to</span> <span m="1972790">pay</span>
  <span m="1972970">you</span> <span m="1973030">back.</span></p><p><span m="1974430">Now,</span>

  <span m="2067969">your</span> <span m="2068030">money</span> <span m="2068179">in</span>
  <span m="2068239">a</span> <span m="2068300">bank.</span> <span m="2068800">But
  when</span> <span m="2068980">you</span> <span m="2069080">put</span> <span m="2069260">your</span>
  <span m="2069350">money</span> <span m="2069560">in</span> <span m="2069620">a</span>
  <span m="2069679">bank,</span> <span m="2070159">you're</span> <span m="2070310">essentially</span>
  <span m="2070790">loaning</span> <span m="2071270">it</span> <span m="2071360">to</span>
  <span m="2071449">companies.</span> <span m="2072409">That's</span> <span m="2072620">essentially</span>
  <span m="2073100">what</span> <span m="2073280">you're</span> <span m="2073370">doing.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2075350">mechanisms,</span> <span m="2076639">we</span> <span m="2076850">have</span>
  <span m="2077060">a</span> <span m="2077150">capital</span> <span m="2077780">market</span>

  <span m="2079460">my</span> <span m="2079820">putting</span> <span m="2080150">money</span>
  <span m="2080420">away</span> <span m="2081739">and</span> <span m="2081830">diverting</span>
  <span m="2082190">from</span> <span m="2082370">today's</span> <span m="2082699">consumption,</span>
  <span m="2083300">I'm</span> <span m="2083540">loaning</span> <span m="2083900">to
  a</span> <span m="2084050">firm.</span> <span m="2084800">They'll</span> <span m="2084949">produce</span>
  <span m="2085250">more,</span> <span m="2085400">and</span> <span m="2085489">they'll</span>
  <span m="2085610">pay</span> <span m="2085790">me</span> <span m="2085909">back</span>
  <span m="2086120">more</span> <span m="2086239">in</span> <span m="2086330">the</span>
  <span m="2086389">future.</span> <span m="2089070">Questions</span> <span m="2089429">about</span>
  <span m="2089610">that?</span></p><p><span m="2091889">OK,</span> <span m="2092280">so</span>
  <span m="2092460">let's</span> <span m="2092699">talk</span> <span m="2092909">about</span>
  <span m="2093060">where the</span> <span m="2093120">supply</span> <span m="2093449">curve</span>
  <span m="2094199">comes</span> <span m="2094500">from.</span> <span m="2095170">We</span>
  <span m="2095190">know</span> <span m="2095389">where</span> <span m="2095520">the</span>
  <span m="2095560">demand</span> <span m="2095670">curve</span> <span m="2096000">comes</span>
  <span m="2096239">from.</span> <span m="2096920">It</span> <span m="2097080">just</span>
  <span m="2097230">simply</span> <span m="2097530">comes</span> <span m="2097800">from</span>
  <span m="2097860">the</span> <span m="2097950">marginal</span> <span m="2098280">revenue</span>
  <span m="2098520">product</span> <span m="2098620">of</span> <span m="2098850">capital.</span></p><p><span
  m="2100350">Where does</span> <span m="2100650">supply</span> <span m="2101040">curve</span>
  <span m="2101280">comes</span> <span m="2101460">from?</span> <span m="2101940">The</span>
  <span m="2102060">supply</span> <span m="2102510">curve</span> <span m="2103350">comes</span>
  <span m="2103830">from</span> <span m="2105240">what</span> <span m="2105390">we</span>
  <span m="2105570">call</span> <span m="2106830">intertemporal</span> <span m="2107700">choice.</span>
  <span m="2111870">As</span> <span m="2112080">I</span> <span m="2112140">said,</span>
  <span m="2112320">economists</span> <span m="2112710">like</span> <span m="2112860">putting</span>
  <span m="2113080">fancy</span> <span m="2113490">names</span> <span m="2113820">on</span>
  <span m="2113940">things.</span> <span m="2115020">That</span> <span m="2115800">helps</span>
  <span m="2116070">us</span> <span m="2116190">get</span> <span m="2116400">paid</span>
  <span m="2116640">more</span> <span m="2116790">money.</span> <span m="2117840">It</span>
  <span m="2117930">just</span> <span m="2118110">means</span> <span m="2118320">choosing</span>

  <span m="2121070">choice.</span> <span m="2121760">Intertemporal</span> <span m="2122300">choice</span>
  <span m="2122930">is</span> <span m="2123110">essentially</span> <span m="2123650">about</span>
  <span m="2124400">how</span> <span m="2124760">do</span> <span m="2124850">you</span>
  <span m="2124940">decide</span> <span m="2125300">how</span> <span m="2125420">much</span>
  <span m="2125660">to</span> <span m="2125750">save.</span> <span m="2127280">What's</span>
  <span m="2127610">going</span> <span m="2127730">to</span> <span m="2127790">determine</span>
  <span m="2128270">that</span> <span m="2129260">is</span> <span m="2129410">going</span>
  <span m="2129530">to</span> <span m="2129620">be</span> <span m="2129740">your</span>
  <span m="2129980">decision</span> <span m="2130850">of</span> <span m="2131000">how</span>
  <span m="2131240">much</span> <span m="2131570">you</span> <span m="2131690">value</span>
  <span m="2132150">money</span> <span m="2132290">today</span> <span m="2133610">versus</span>
  <span m="2133970">valuing</span> <span m="2134360">money</span> <span m="2134600">tomorrow.</span></p><p><span
  m="2137710">So</span> <span m="2138130">for</span> <span m="2138370">ease,</span>
  <span m="2139120">let's</span> <span m="2139360">imagine</span> <span m="2139810">I'm</span>
  <span m="2139900">considering</span> <span m="2140350">two</span> <span m="2140560">periods,</span>
  <span m="2140980">this</span> <span m="2141160">year</span> <span m="2141280">versus</span>
  <span m="2141580">next</span> <span m="2141850">year.</span> <span m="2142780">When</span>
  <span m="2142900">I</span> <span m="2142960">talk</span> <span m="2143110">about</span>
  <span m="2143220">periods,</span> <span m="2143450">I'm talking</span> <span m="2143590">about</span>
  <span m="2143740">days</span> <span m="2144100">and</span> <span m="2144190">years</span>
  <span m="2144560">and</span> <span m="2144660">whatever.</span> <span m="2145450">It's</span>
  <span m="2145600">the</span> <span m="2145690">basic</span> <span m="2145990">logic.</span>
  <span m="2146380">It's about</span> <span m="2146560">now</span> <span m="2146860">versus</span>
  <span m="2147100">the</span> <span m="2147190">future.</span> <span m="2147680">Whether

  <span m="2584450">substitution</span> <span m="2584900">effect</span> <span m="2585100">says</span>
  <span m="2585290">you</span> <span m="2585380">do</span> <span m="2585530">less</span>
  <span m="2585770">of</span> <span m="2585860">it.</span></p><p><span m="2587410">But</span>
  <span m="2587940">if</span> <span m="2588170">interest</span> <span m="2588420">rate</span>

  <span m="2589530">richer.</span> <span m="2591010">And</span> <span m="2591130">if</span>

  <span m="2604990">other.</span></p><p><span m="2605300">Let's</span> <span m="2605410">look</span>
